GT Equivalence Verification (PO24)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - alpha*v**c0 - beta*log(Abs(v) + c1)
Candidate formulas: 60

GT (fixed):
\[
f(t,v)=0.782414626093252\sin t\;-\;0.0834249779987997\,v^3\;-\;0.995417005601056\log(|v|+1).
\]
So we need exactly: one pure \(\sin(t)\) term (no extra \(t\)-dependence), one \(v^3\) term, and one \(\log(|v|+1)\) term, with no additional nonzero terms. Candidate parameters may be set to 0 to delete extra terms. Also \(\log(c\cdot |v|+1)\) must match \(\log(|v|+1)\), which forces \(c=1\) (since \(\log(a|v|+1)\neq \log(|v|+1)\) for all \(v\) unless \(a=1\)).

Below, for each candidate, I check whether we can (i) kill extra terms by setting coefficients to 0, (ii) match \(\sin(t)\) up to phase/frequency, and (iii) match the \(v\)-terms.

1. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^3+c4\log(c5|v|+1)+c6 e^{c7|v|}\sin(c8 t+c9)\)  
   Set \(c6=0\). Then match with \(c1=1,c2=0,c0=0.7824\); \(c3=-0.083425\); \(c4=-0.995417\); \(c5=1\). Works. **Match**.

2. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\sin(c4 t+c5)+c6 v^3+c7\log(c8|v|+1)\)  
   Set \(c3=0\). Then same matching as above with \(c1=1,c2=0,c0=0.7824\); \(c6=-0.083425\); \(c7=-0.995417\); \(c8=1\). **Match**.

3. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^3+c4\log(c5|v|+1)+c6\exp(c7\sin(c8 t+c9))\)  
   The last term depends on \(t\) nonlinearly; set \(c6=0\). Remaining terms can match exactly as in (1). **Match**.

4. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^3+c4\log(c5|v|+1)+c6 v e^{c7|v|}\cos(c8 t+c9)\)  
   Extra mixed \(t,v\) term; set \(c6=0\). Remaining matches. **Match**.

5. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^3+c4\log(c5|v|+1)+c6\log(c7|v|+1)\cos(c8 t+c9)\)  
   Extra \(t\)-dependent factor; set \(c6=0\). Remaining matches. **Match**.

6. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v\sin(c4 t+c5)^2+c6 v^3+c7\log(c8|v|+1)+c9 v\)  
   Need no \(v\) or \(v\cdot(\text{time})\) terms: set \(c3=0\) and \(c9=0\). Then match \(\sin\), \(v^3\), \(\log\) as usual with \(c1=1,c2=0\), \(c6=-0.083425\), \(c7=-0.995417\), \(c8=1\). **Match**.

7. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 v^3+c5\log(c6|v|+1)+c7 v\cos(c8 t+c9)\)  
   Set \(c3=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match remaining. **Match**.

8. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^{c4}+c5+c6 v^3+c7\log(c8|v|+1)\)

9. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 v^3+c5\log(c6|v|+1)+c7 v e^{c8|v|}\)  
   Set \(c3=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match remaining. **Match**.

10. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 v^3+c5\log(c6|v|+1)+c7\log(c8 e^{c9 v}+1)\)  
   Extra \(\log(c8 e^{c9 v}+1)\) depends on signed \(v\) (not \(|v|\)) and cannot become constant for all \(v\) unless \(c7=0\). Set \(c7=0\), \(c3=0\). Then match remaining. **Match**.

11. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 v^3+c5\log(c6|v|+1)+c7 v\)  
   Set \(c3=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match remaining. **Match**.

   Extra \(e^{c4 v}\) term: set \(c3=0\). Also set \(c5=0\). Then match remaining. **Match**.

13. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v|v|+c4 v^3+c5\log(c6|v|+1)+c7 v\)  
   GT has no \(v|v|\) or \(v\): set \(c3=0\), \(c7=0\). Then match with \(c4=-0.083425\), \(c5=-0.995417\), \(c6=1\), and \(\sin\) parameters. **Match**.

15. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^{c4}+c5 v^3+c6\log(c7|v|+1)\)

18. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 v^3+c5\log(c6|v|+1)\)

23. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\sin(c4 v+c5)+c6 v^3+c7\log(c8|v|+1)\)  
   Extra \(\sin(\text{function of }v)\): set \(c3=0\). Then match remaining. **Match**.

24. Same as 23 plus constant \(c6\) (here written as \(+c6\) and \(+c7 v^3\) etc.)  
   Set the constant term to 0 and the \(\sin(v)\) term to 0: \(c3=0\), (constant) \(c6=0\). Then match \(v^3\) and \(\log\) and \(\sin(t)\). **Match**.

25. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^3+c4 v+c5 v^3+c6\log(c7|v|+1)\)  
   Need no linear \(v\): set \(c4=0\). Combine \(v^3\) coefficients: choose \(c3+c5=-0.083425\). Set \(c6=-0.995417\), \(c7=1\), and \(\sin\) match. **Match**.

26. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^2+c4 v^{c5}+c6 e^{c7 v}\log(c8|v|+1)\)  
   GT needs \(v^3\) and plain \(\log\) (not multiplied by \(e^{c7 v}\)). You could set \(c6=0\) to remove the log entirely, but then you cannot reproduce the required log term. If instead keep \(c6\neq 0\), to make \(e^{c7 v}\) constant for all \(v\) requires \(c7=0\), giving \(c6\log(c8|v|+1)\) which is fine. But then you still must eliminate \(v^2\) and match \(v^3\) via \(c4 v^{c5}\): set \(c3=0\), set \(c5=3\), \(c4=-0.083425\). Also set \(c6=-0.995417\), \(c7=0\), \(c8=1\). Then \(\sin\) matches. **Match**.

27. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^2+c4+c5 v^{c6}+c7 e^{c8 v}\log(c9|v|+1)\)  
   Set \(c4=0\), \(c3=0\). Make exponential constant: \(c8=0\). Then choose \(c6=3\), \(c5=-0.083425\). Set \(c7=-0.995417\), \(c9=1\). \(\sin\) matches. **Match**.

30. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v v^{c4}+c5+c6 v^3+c7\log(c8|v|+1)+c9 v\)  
   Note \(v v^{c4}=v^{c4+1}\) (problematic for negative \(v\) if non-integer exponent; but we can avoid it). Set \(c3=0\), \(c5=0\), \(c9=0\). Then match with \(c6=-0.083425\), \(c7=-0.995417\), \(c8=1\), and \(\sin\). **Match**.

33. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^3+c4 v^3+c5\log(c6|v|+1)\)

34. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^2+c4 v^{c5}+c6\sin(c7\log(c8|v|+1)+c9)\)  
   The last term is \(\sin(\log(\cdot))\), not present in GT; set \(c6=0\). Then set \(c3=0\), choose \(c5=3\), \(c4=-0.083425\). But now there is no log term at all, so cannot match GT. If keep \(c6\neq 0\), \(\sin(c7\log(\cdot)+c9)\) cannot equal a linear \(\log(\cdot)\) for all \(v\). **No match**.

35. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3+c4 v^3+c5\log(c6|v|+1)+c7 v^{c8}e^{c9 v}\)  
   Extra term: set \(c7=0\), set \(c3=0\). Then match remaining. **Match**.

36. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 e^{c4 t}+c5+c6 v^3+c7\log(c8|v|+1)\)  
   Extra \(e^{c4 t}\) and constant: set \(c3=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match remaining. **Match**.

37. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3 v^3+c4\log(c5|v|+1)+c6\cos(c7 e^{c8 t})\)  
   Extra \(\cos(c7 e^{c8 t})\) cannot be made identically 0 except by setting \(c6=0\). Do so, then match remaining. **Match**.

38. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\sin(c4+c5\log(c6|v|+1))+c7 v^3\)  
   To remove the \(\sin(\log)\) term set \(c3=0\), but then there is no log term at all, so cannot match GT. Keeping it cannot equal \(\log(|v|+1)\) globally. **No match**.

39. \(c0\sin(c1 t+c2)+c3\log(c4 v+1)+c5+c6 v^3+c7\log(c8|v|+1)\)  
   \(\log(c4 v+1)\) depends on signed \(v\) and has domain issues for negative \(v\); GT uses \(\log(|v|+1)\). Best is set \(c3=0\), \(c5=0\). Then match with \(c6=-0.083425\), \(c7=-0.995417\), \(c8=1\), and \(\sin\). **Match**.
